           <div class="details-section-contents show-more-container" data-show-height="144" data-show-use-buffer="true"> 
            <h1 aria-label="Description"></h1> 
            <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description"> 
             <div class="id-app-orig-desc">
              FRUIT NINJA 5TH ANNIVERSARY SPECIAL: The Fruit Ninjas are celebrating 5 fun, fruity, and fantastic years with 50% off the premium 75 Rubies pack! We’ve also added an exclusive hidden reward for ninjas on Google Play. Get your throwing stars ready, there’s no excuse to miss this!
              <p>Feel the rush and hold on tight as you rappel down mountains at breakneck speed.</p>
              <p>Pull off death-defying tricks by ricocheting between launch pads, riding rainbows and rocketing over obstacles in the most redonkulous adventure ever.</p>
              <p>Rack up coins and complete rockin’ missions to unlock sweet new gear for Rip and Roxy, the most fearless risk-takers on the planet.</p>
              <p>It’s random. It’s ridiculous. It’s really, really rad. Play for FREE now!</p>
              <p>*****</p>
              <p>RIP &amp; ROXY<br>Choose your favourite rappeller, each with unique quests and collectibles!</p>
              <p>RIGHTEOUS TRICKS<br>Raise the bar with a huge range of heart-stopping tricks and epic manoeuvres!</p>
              <p>RANDOMIZER<br>Roll the Randomizer to equip game-changing power-ups like Recoil Boots and Revives!</p>
              <p>RADICAL REMIX<br>Chain tricks and maintain momentum to fill the Remix Bar and become invincible!</p>
              <p>RAGING RIVALRIES<br>Compete against friends to cement your spot as the craziest thrill-seeker on the planet!</p>
              <p>*****</p>
              <p>IMPORTANT NOTICE:</p>
              <p>This game contains optional in-app purchases. You can disable this feature in the settings menu of your device.</p>
              <p>View our privacy policy at <a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttp://halfbrick.com/pp%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNFeVipjQR1-YroLf3t-dyHT4YhAfw&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNE-F42MBCu3qGaVe2YB_-U5VnUhCA" target="_blank">http://halfbrick.com/pp</a><br>View our terms of service at <a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttp://halfbrick.com/tos%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNHfBMA6PtiP5z8G5F3BbtFl5mFb5Q&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNE0whsRPh8oNSIEK6n1qFwU_ecr0A" target="_blank">http://halfbrick.com/tos</a></p>
